                         570,  'MB_2',

                        ];
        var widgetID = formatToWidget[formatToWidget.length-1];
        for (w = 0; w &lt; formatToWidget.length; w++) {
            if (formatToWidget[w] &gt;= viewportMaxSide) {
                widgetID = formatToWidget[w+1];
                break;
            }
        }

        var plh = 'www';

            The full moon, nicknamed "the supermoon", rises at Ipanema beach in Rio de Janeiro, Brazil, on August 10, 2014. A supermoon is the coincidence of a full moon or a new moon with the closest approach the Moon makes to the Earth on its elliptical orbit, resulting in the largest apparent size of the lunar disk as seen from Earth.         <script type="text/javascript">
         jQuery(function(){
                $("#modal_signin_close").on("click",function(){
                    $('#modal_signin_div').hide();
                    return false;
                });
                $('#modal_signin_div .checkbox-div').on("click",function(){
                    if ($(this).text() == "X") {
                        $(this).text("");
                        $('#modal_signin_rememberme').removeAttr('checked');
                    } else {
                        $(this).text("X");
                        $('#modal_signin_rememberme').attr('checked', 'checked');
                    }
                    return false;
                });
                try {$('input, textarea').placeholder();} catch (e) {}
            });
        </script>

    <!-- templates/hearst/home/viafouraFooterJS.tpl -->
    <script>
     // This must be correctly defined before Viafoura is called
    // or else we run the risk of tainting the comments for a particular url
    $('meta[property="og:url"]').attr('content', location.href);
    
    
    
    (function (v, s) {
        v.type = 'text/javascript';
        v.async = !0;
        v.src = location.protocol !== 'https:' ? '//cdn.viafoura.net/vf.js' : '//api.viafoura.com/app/js/vf.js';
        s.parentNode.insertBefore(v, s)
    }(document.createElement('script'), document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0]));

    $(document).ready(function () {
        if ($('#hdn-vf-comments').length) {HDN.authOnReady('free',true)}
        var vfDomains = {};
        $('body').find('div.viafoura span.vf-counter[data-path^="http://"]').each(function () {
            var matches = $(this).attr('data-path').match(/^https?\:\/\/([^\/?#]+)(?:[\/?#]|$)/i);
            var domain = matches &amp;&amp; matches[1];
            if (!!domain) {
                vfDomains[domain.replace(/^m\./, 'www.')] = 1;
            }
        });
        for (d in vfDomains) {
            HDN.getVfCommentCount(undefined,d,1);
        }
    });
    </script>
